#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_activities
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_activities;

CREATE TABLE `bf_activities` (
  `activity_id` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` bigint(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `activity` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `module` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `created_on` datetime NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`activity_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=112 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_catalog_settings
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_catalog_settings;

CREATE TABLE `bf_catalog_settings` (
  `id` int(10) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `title` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `value` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `pos` tinyint(2) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `name` (`name`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=6 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

INSERT INTO bf_catalog_settings (`id`, `name`, `title`, `value`, `pos`) VALUES (1, 'title', 'Заголовок каталога', 'Каталог товаров', 1);
INSERT INTO bf_catalog_settings (`id`, `name`, `title`, `value`, `pos`) VALUES (2, 'deep', 'Глубина вложенности (макс. 5)', '5', 2);
INSERT INTO bf_catalog_settings (`id`, `name`, `title`, `value`, `pos`) VALUES (3, 'previmagesize', 'Размеры картинки превью', '100x150', 3);
INSERT INTO bf_catalog_settings (`id`, `name`, `title`, `value`, `pos`) VALUES (4, 'largeimagesize', 'Размеры большой картинки', '400x400', 4);
INSERT INTO bf_catalog_settings (`id`, `name`, `title`, `value`, `pos`) VALUES (5, 'upload_dir', 'Папка для загрузки картинок', '/files/uploads/catalog', 5);


#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_catalogs
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_catalogs;

CREATE TABLE `bf_catalogs` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `title` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `parent_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `pos` tinyint(2) NOT NULL,
  `deleted` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `hidden` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `parent_id` (`parent_id`),
  KEY `pos` (`pos`),
  KEY `deleted` (`deleted`),
  KEY `hidden` (`hidden`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=26 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

INSERT INTO bf_catalogs (`id`, `title`, `parent_id`, `pos`, `deleted`, `hidden`) VALUES (20, 'Машины', 0, 3, 0, 0);

# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_datastores
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_datastores;

CREATE TABLE `bf_datastores` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `page_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `extformtable_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `extformtable_record_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `ds_type` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `field_value` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `pos` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `base_url` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `per_page` int(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '20',
  `uri_segment` int(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '3',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `page_id` (`page_id`),
  KEY `extformtable_id` (`extformtable_id`),
  KEY `extformtable_record_id` (`extformtable_record_id`),
  KEY `ds_type` (`ds_type`),
  KEY `pos` (`pos`),
  KEY `name` (`name`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=9 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_email_queue
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_email_queue;

CREATE TABLE `bf_email_queue` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `to_email` varchar(128) NOT NULL,
  `subject` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `message` text NOT NULL,
  `alt_message` text,
  `max_attempts` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '3',
  `attempts` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `success` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `date_published` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `last_attempt` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `date_sent` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

Ответственность за взрывы взяла на себя нигерийская исламистская террористическая группировка <em>\"Боко Харам\"</em>.</span> <a class=\"source\" href=\"http://www.interfax.ru/society/news.asp?id=223713\" target=\"_blank\">Интерфакс</a> <span class=\"time\">&nbsp;16:52</span></p>\r\n<p class=\"text\"><span>В результате пяти взрывов, совершенных в Рождественское воскресенье у христианских церквей в различных городах Нигерии, погибли, по меньшей мере, 25 человек. # TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_formtable_newsphotos
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_formtable_newsphotos;

CREATE TABLE `bf_formtable_newsphotos` (
  `id` int(11) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `photoname` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `photofile` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `title` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=5 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_groups
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_groups;

CREATE TABLE `bf_groups` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `name` (`name`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=4 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

INSERT INTO bf_groups (`id`, `name`) VALUES (1, 'Administrator');
INSERT INTO bf_groups (`id`, `name`) VALUES (2, 'Moderator');
INSERT INTO bf_groups (`id`, `name`) VALUES (3, 'Member');


#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_infoparams
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_infoparams;

CREATE TABLE `bf_infoparams` (
  `id` int(10) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` char(50) NOT NULL,
  `title` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `table_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `fieldtype` int(10) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `name` (`name`),
  KEY `table_id` (`table_id`),
  KEY `fieldtype` (`fieldtype`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=5 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

INSERT INTO bf_infoparams (`id`, `name`, `title`, `table_id`, `fieldtype`) VALUES (1, 'name', 'Заголовок', 1, 1);
INSERT INTO bf_infoparams (`id`, `name`, `title`, `table_id`, `fieldtype`) VALUES (2, 'descr', 'Краткое описание', 1, 3);
INSERT INTO bf_infoparams (`id`, `name`, `title`, `table_id`, `fieldtype`) VALUES (3, 'text', 'Полный текст', 1, 6);
INSERT INTO bf_infoparams (`id`, `name`, `title`, `table_id`, `fieldtype`) VALUES (4, 'date_open', 'Дата создания', 1, 7);


#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_infoparamtypes
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_infoparamtypes;

CREATE TABLE `bf_infoparamtypes` (
  `id` int(10) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `title` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `fieldtype` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `valuetype` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `fieldtype` (`fieldtype`),
  KEY `valuetype` (`valuetype`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=8 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

INSERT INTO bf_infoparamtypes (`id`, `title`, `fieldtype`, `valuetype`) VALUES (1, 'Text', 'text', 'text');

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_infoparamvalues
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_infoparamvalues;

CREATE TABLE `bf_infoparamvalues` (
  `id` int(10) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `param_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `value` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `param_id` (`param_id`),
  KEY `value` (`value`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_inforecordgroups
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_inforecordgroups;

CREATE TABLE `bf_inforecordgroups` (
  `id` int(10) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `title` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `table_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `table_id` (`table_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_inforecords
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_inforecords;

CREATE TABLE `bf_inforecords` (
  `id` bigint(50) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `table_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `hidden` tinyint(1) NOT NULL,
  `group_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `user_id` (`user_id`),
  KEY `table_id` (`table_id`),
  KEY `group_id` (`group_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_inforecordvalues
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_inforecordvalues;

CREATE TABLE `bf_inforecordvalues` (
  `id` int(10) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `param_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `table_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `record_id` bigint(50) NOT NULL,
  `charvalue` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `textvalue` text NOT NULL,
  `intvalue` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `bigtextvalue` longtext NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `param_id` (`param_id`),
  KEY `table_id` (`table_id`),
  KEY `charvalue` (`charvalue`),
  KEY `intvalue` (`intvalue`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_infotables
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_infotables;

CREATE TABLE `bf_infotables` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `user_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `user_id` (`user_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=2 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

INSERT INTO bf_infotables (`id`, `name`, `user_id`) VALUES (1, 'Пасспорт ОСИ', 0);


#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_login_attempts
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_login_attempts;

CREATE TABLE `bf_login_attempts` (
  `id` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `ip_address` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `login` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `time` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=6 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_pages
#

  `id` int(10) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,

  `tplID` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `keywords` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `active` tinyint(1) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=6 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_recfiles
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_recfiles;

CREATE TABLE `bf_recfiles` (
  `id` bigint(50) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `tableID` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `recordID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `path` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `ext` varchar(10) NOT NULL,
  `size` double NOT NULL,
  `fieldID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `tableID` (`tableID`),
  KEY `recordID` (`recordID`),
  KEY `fieldID` (`fieldID`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=11 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_user_cookies
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_user_cookies;

CREATE TABLE `bf_user_cookies` (
  `user_id` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `token` varchar(128) NOT NULL,
  `created_on` datetime NOT NULL,
  KEY `token` (`token`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_users
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_users;

CREATE TABLE `bf_users` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `role_id` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '4',
  `first_name` varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `last_name` varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `email` varchar(120) NOT NULL,
  `username` varchar(30) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `password_hash` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `reset_hash` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `salt` varchar(7) NOT NULL,
  `last_login` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `last_ip` varchar(40) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `created_on` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `street_1` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `street_2` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `city` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `zipcode` varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleted` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `reset_by` int(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  `country_iso` char(2) DEFAULT 'US',
  `state_code` char(4) DEFAULT '',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `email` (`email`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=6 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;
